For my dissertation, I am studying Acculturative stress and factors that impact individual\u2019s adaptation. I am conducting research with international students from sub-Sahara Africa due to the lack of research for this population. Data will be collected for this research through the internet, via Survey Monkey \u2122. \n\nYour feedback is very important to me. As the researcher, your information is confidential and I will not have access to your personal information. The information and data collected and reported will be used only in my dissertation; is completely anonymous; and will not include participant names, e-mail addresses, and/or personal Internet identifiers. Survey Monkey.com \u2122 allows researchers to suppress the delivery of IP addresses during the downloading of data. In this study, no IP address will be delivered to this researcher. \n\nThe Survey Monkey \u2122 platform prevents the researcher from acquiring any identifying or personal information from the participant\u2019s use of the platform. However, Survey Monkey \u2122 does collect IP addresses for its own purposes. If you have concerns about this, you should review the privacy policy of Survey Monkey \u2122 before you begin. \n\nYour consent to be a research participant in this study is strictly voluntary, and should you decline to participate or should you choose to drop out at any time during this study, there will be no adverse effects. Moreover, no monetary compensation from participating in this study will be received. \n\nIf you choose to participate in this research study, you will be asked to do the following:\n\n1.) Read the Informed Consent for participation in this research study, which is found online when you open the survey. \n\n2.) Confirm your participation in this research study or decline to participate in this study. If you decline to participate you will simply exit the survey. If you choose to participate, your anonymity will be protected at all times.\n\n3.) Respond to a series of survey questions.   \n\nThank you for your time and consideration.
